Frequently Asked Questions

What is the PluginRegistration subdomain?
PluginRegistration is a subdomain in the spring-boot codebase, part of the GradlePlugin domain. Reactive application of logic when Java or Application plugins are applied. It contains 0 source files.
Which domain does PluginRegistration belong to?
PluginRegistration belongs to the GradlePlugin domain.
What functions are in PluginRegistration?
The PluginRegistration subdomain contains 14108 function(s): AbandonedRunException, AbstractBindHandler, AbstractBootArchiveIntegrationTests, AbstractBootArchiveTests, AbstractCommand, AbstractDependsOnBeanFactoryPostProcessor, AbstractFilterRegistrationBean, AbstractLoggingSystem, and 14100 more.
